Some activities also make the learners think about the meaning of the words in the context of a sentence—a sentence different from the sentences that occurred in the introduction of the words. Moreover, each unit ends with a story containing the target words. While reading the story, the learners have to recall the meanings of the words and suit them to the context of the story. Such activities help learners develop a better understanding of a common meaning for a given word which fits the different uses.\r\n\r\nIllustrations for each target word are provided to help learners visualize the word as it is being used in the example sentence. However, this series focuses on the word’s most common form.
